If the trump is chosen in the first round you receive the trump card and must shed any card you wish.\r\n‚úì\tThe player next to the dealer in a clock-wise direction is the first to choose a trump suit. \r\n‚úì\tIf that player passes the chance, the next one after him follows.\r\n‚úì\tThe game is played between two teams: a top-bottom team comprised of you and a computer player and a left-right team of computer players.\r\n‚úì\tThe player and his partner are called the makers if one of them chooses a trump suit. Otherwise they are called the defenders.\r\n‚úì\tTo win the makers must take at least 3 tricks. The defenders in order to win must take at least 3 tricks as well.\r\n‚úì\tIf the makers take 5 tricks they score 2 points. If the defenders take 3 or more tricks they score 2 points.\r\n‚úì\tIf the makers take 3 or 4 tricks they score 1 point. If the makers take less than 3 tricks they score 0 points.\r\n‚úì\tThere is the possibility of playing alone by pressing the -play alone- button when choosing the trump.\r\n‚úì\tWhen playing alone the team scores 4 points if the maker takes all 5 tricks. Otherwise if the team takes 3 or 4 tricks it scores only 1 point.\r\n‚úì\tThere is a specific order of the trump cards. The trump Jack is the most valuable card, followed by the Jack of the same-color suit. \r\n‚úì\tFor example if the trump suit is hearts, the most valuable card is the Jack of hearts followed by the Jack of diamonds.\r\n‚úì\tThese cards are followed by the Ace, the King, the Queen, the 10 and the 9. \r\n‚úì\tThere are only 24 cards in the deck - 6 from each suit.\r\n‚úì\tThe order of the cards in the other suits is the Ace, the King, the Queen, the Jack, the 10 and the 9.\r\n‚úì\tThe Jack of the same color as the trump suit makes part of the trump suit.\r\n‚úì\tYou can start the trick with any card but you must follow suit or play any other card if you cannot follow suit.\r\n‚úì\tThe trick is won by the player who plays the highest trump or the highest card of the starting suit.\r\n‚úì\tTo win the game you must be the first to score 10 or more points.\r\n‚úì\tThere is a statistics menu in which you can view the total games played, the percentage of won games, the number of rounds played, the number of euchres made.\r\n‚úì\tIf you as a defender take 3 or more tricks then you achieve a euchre.\r\n‚úì\tIf you as a maker take less than 3 tricks then you have been euchred.\r\n‚úì\tThe makers are marked with an M.
